  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8dcf2212-01e1-4b2a-b40f-affc3bc8f762'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText2688879937984858675" style="display:none"><b>Too hot to handle...</b><br /><br />Tabitha Allen grew up in the thick of Chaos—the Chaos Motorcycle Club, that is. Her father is Chaos' leader, and the club has always had her back. But one rider was different from the start. When Tabby was running wild, Shy Cage was there. When tragedy tore her life apart, he helped her piece it back together. And now, Tabby's thinking about much more than friendship...<br /><br />Tabby is everything Shy's ever wanted, but everything he thinks he can't have. She's beautiful, smart, and as his friend's daughter, untouchable. Shy never expected more than friendship, so when Tabby indicates she wants more—<i>much </i>more<i>—</i>he feels like the luckiest man alive. But even lucky men can crash and burn...</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">According to another Goodreads member, Kristen Ashley posted on her website that Rush is getting his own story but it hasn't been developed yet. Appar<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">According to another Goodreads member, Kristen Ashley posted on her website that Rush is getting his own story but it hasn't been developed yet. Apparently, Rush's story will be the last story in the Chaos MC series but there's no indication how many more books KA plans to write for this series before Rush's "finale." I'm waiting with baited breath for Rush's story, too :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer465076721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1505536137841628245"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399007i/771649._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <i> I ABSOLUTELY FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK!!!!!!!! </i> <br/><br/>No word of a lie: I have quotes highlighted on nearly EVERY page of this book!!<br/><br/>Kristen Ashley is one of those incredibly talented authors who has my complete and utter trust. I don’t need to read the synopsis or blurbs for her books, I don’t need to see reviews or ratings… Quite simply, if she wrote it, I’ll read it.<br/><br/>And true to KA style, this book ROCKED. MY. WORLD. </b><br/><br/>First, I just want to say that although technically this book can be read as a sta</span>
  <span id="freeText1505536137841628245" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399007i/771649._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> I ABSOLUTELY FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK!!!!!!!! </i> <br><br>No word of a lie: I have quotes highlighted on nearly EVERY page of this book!!<br><br>Kristen Ashley is one of those incredibly talented authors who has my complete and utter trust. I don’t need to read the synopsis or blurbs for her books, I don’t need to see reviews or ratings… Quite simply, if she wrote it, I’ll read it.<br><br>And true to KA style, this book ROCKED. MY. WORLD. </b><br><br>First, I just want to say that although technically this book can be read as a standalone, if you haven’t yet read the Dream Man series, you are going to miss out on a good chunk of the emotional impact of it. And to clarify: you’ll definitely feel the romance between Shy and Tabby for sure either way, but in order to get the full EPICNESS that this book has to offer (and trust me, there’s bucket-loads of epic!), you really have to read them after the Dream Man books. There are cameos from Tack, Tyra, Hawk, Elvira, Brock and Mitch, as well as Lee Nightingale, Tex and Fortums (from Rock Chick) so if those names don’t mean anything to you, their scenes won’t send you into the same squee-ing frenzy that they sent me into. So yeah, I suggest reading the Dream Man books first (click here for the full reading order).<br><br>Ok, on to the review ;)<br><br>Parker “Shy” Cage has a bit of a reputation. One involving copious piles of women. Ok, hang on, let’s just take a collective moment to SWOON over his name. I’m in love with it. I’m in love with him. *dreamy sigh*… Ok, moving on. Yeah, let’s just say he’s gotten around. A lot And to say that he and Tabby got off to a rocky start would be the understatement of the year.<br><br>As the daughter of the leader of the biker gang Chaos that Shy was a brother in, Tabby was off-limits to begin with. But when he sees her going down a path he thinks is bad for her, he decides to try and teach her a lesson. His intentions were good, but his delivery… not so much. His point goes through but he went too far and the hurt ran deep. And for the next few years, she can barely stand the sight of him.<br><br>But when a tragedy shatters Tabby’s world, Shy is there to help her put back the pieces and learn to be happy again. (And stop freaking out guys, Tack does NOT die!! Breathe. It’s okay!)<br><br><i> <b> “You need a safe place to just forget shit and escape, I’ll give it to you. Tonight. Tomorrow. Next week. Next month. That safe place is me, Tabby.” </b></i> <br><br>I totally loved both Shy and Tabby. Once they got past the initial misunderstandings and miss-communications and officially became a couple, my gosh were they ever functional!!! They were crazy in love and both valued what they had more than anything else in the world. It was precious to them and they weren’t about to let anything get in their way or come between them. They knew where their priorities lay and it was their relationship first. Above all else. I just absolutely freaking ADORED them as a couple!!<br><br><i> <b> “Promise me right now, my dick still inside you, you naked on top of me in my bed, sharing what we just shared, us having a taste of what it’s like apart and knowin’ were better together, you won’t leave me…. You’ll stick with me until there’s nothing to stick to, if that ever happens.” </b></i> <br><br>And as individual characters, they were both also amazing. Tabby was just incredible. She spoke her mind, stood up for herself and didn’t take shit from anyone (and considering that she was always surrounded by these badass biker dudes, that was quite a feat).<br><br>And Shy just stole my heart because despite royally fucking up in the beginning, he was the kind of guy who could own up to it, apologize, and move on. He was Alpha, protected and defended his woman, but at the same time wasn’t overbearing and loved her for who she was – the good and the bad.<br><br>I loved that despite the way the older bikers ran things, Shy, I guess being younger (27) and maybe more open to change was a biker through and through but at the same time, didn’t put up with a lot of the older ways of dealing with relationships. He had a lot of respect for Tabby in her own right and didn’t let anyone get in her way.<br><br><i> <b> “Shy, she’s yours… Control your woman,” High demanded. “Get her ass out.” <br><br>My eyes went to Shy to see him looking at High, and he wasn’t looking pissed.<br><br>He was looking reflective.<br><br>Then he said, “Tab and I don’t play it that way. You wanna order your old lady around, do what you do, not for me to say. I asked her to go, she didn’t go. Not gonna make her. But you try, you’ll deal with me.” </b></i> <br><br>This book was tight. The story flowed, it was engaging, something new was always happening and there were no dull moments. The imagery was vivid – I honestly feel like I saw the whole book play out in front of my eyes like a movie.<br><br>This story had a bit of everything. There were moments that warmed my heart right down to my toes, moments that had me fanning myself and moments that socked me in the gut so hard it took me breath away.<br><br>I really felt like the message that came through to me from this book was that the shit life sometimes puts you through can cut deep, right into your soul. But sometimes, if you push through it, you can find beauty you’d never have otherwise found.<br><br>I swear to God, KA’s writing has just SO much depth to it. She’s very much got her own style and let me tell you: that woman can WRITE. Brilliant dialogue. Scenes that make your heart squeeze and race. Scenes that make you sigh dreamily and just feel like you are right freaking THERE.<br><br>And seriously, this book has one of the most epic verbal smackdowns I have ever read. I was cheering and squeeing. It had some of the best lines from any KA book I’ve ever read (and I’ve nearly read them all). I swear I highlighted almost that whole chapter!!<br><br>And boy was this book HOT! When the main couple have a connection as strong as Shy and Tabby had, you can’t help but feel it. Again, EPIC.<br><br><i> <b> “I knew this day would turn shit,” I whispered. “I knew with how great it started, there’d be farther to fall.”<br><br>His eyes flashed, his hand moved up to cup my jaw, he tilted my head way back, and brought his face to mine.<br><br>“May feel like you’re fallin’, Tabby, but remember, I’m at the bottom ready to catch you.” </b></i> <br><br>It seriously took all my will power not to just post updates every 2 minutes screaming “I FREAKING LOVE THIS BOOK!!!”<br><br>My only tiny complaint was that the epilogue was shorter than most and I do love me a big long gushy epilogue, but still... the book rocked! <br><br>Aaand also, on a bit more of a random note…. what’s better than a hot-as-fuck badass biker?? Well that would be a hot-as-fuck bad ass biker with a smokin’ hot soldier brother. I totally crushed on Shy’s brother, Landon, and really hope he gets his own book one day <br><br>The next installment in this series is well set up and I absolutely can’t wait for MORE!!!!<br><br><u> <b> **SPECIAL (spoiler-free) BONUS SCENE** </b></u> <b><br>For my Blog Tour post, Kristen Ashley wrote a Bonus Scene featuring me "Aestas" and a hot biker dude from Chaos!!! If you want to read it, go to this link:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/book-review-own-the-wind-kristen-ashley/">http://aestasbookblog.com/book-review...</a> </b><br><br><b> *squeeeeee* </b><br><br>5++ stars!!!<br><br>Here is my casting for Shy: <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399007i/771650._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399007i/771651.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399007i/771652._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a> </b><br><br><i> I was provided an ARC in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14137347285061917427"><b>5+ OUTSTANDING stars –Kristen Ashley's best work yet!</b><br/><br/>If I could give this book more than 5 STARS I would. I love</span>
  <span id="freeText14137347285061917427" style="display:none"><b>5+ OUTSTANDING stars –Kristen Ashley's best work yet!</b><br /><br />If I could give this book more than 5 STARS I would. That is how well-crafted and written this story is. I've always loved Kristen Ashley's work and was apprehensive that a professional editor would rob the author of her unique style of storytelling. FOOLISH ME! With a gifted editor, Kristen Ashley has NOW become a ROCK STAR! Kudos to GCP for recognizing a diamond in the rough. <br /><br />To sum it up, I absolutely loved the dynamics of this book. I loved how young Tabby and Shy were, I love the family interactions, and the atypical epilogue. I simply loved this book. <br /><br /><i>**ARC kindly provided to Swept Away By Romance courtesy of Grand Central Publishing, Kristen Ashley and Chas**</i><br />----<br />If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>

<div id="review_479407070" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/479407070" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/479407070?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2018-audio">2018-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479407070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer389349392215624307"><br/><b> 5 Dreamy Stars!!! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/OwntheWind-Idreamedadream_zps693bec26.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778027.jpg' alt=' photo OwntheWind-Idreamedadream_zps693bec26.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>When I started this one, I thought... no way could it be as good as Motorcycle Man and no way could I love Shy and Tabby as much as I loved Tack and Tyra... yeah- I was wrong! I absolutely loved Shy and Tabby is my new favorite KA heroine! <br/><br/>We meet Shy and Tabby in Motorcycle Man. Tabby is Tack’s(Chaos MC’s president’s) daughter, and Shy is a recruit in The Chaos MC. Tabby is young (16) and has a big crush on Shy. Shy is just a few years older than Tabby, but Shy has a repu</span>
  <span id="freeText389349392215624307" style="display:none"><br><b> 5 Dreamy Stars!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/OwntheWind-Idreamedadream_zps693bec26.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778027.jpg" alt=" photo OwntheWind-Idreamedadream_zps693bec26.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When I started this one, I thought... no way could it be as good as Motorcycle Man and no way could I love Shy and Tabby as much as I loved Tack and Tyra... yeah- I was wrong! I absolutely loved Shy and Tabby is my new favorite KA heroine! <br><br>We meet Shy and Tabby in Motorcycle Man. Tabby is Tack’s(Chaos MC’s president’s) daughter, and Shy is a recruit in The Chaos MC. Tabby is young (16) and has a big crush on Shy. Shy is just a few years older than Tabby, but Shy has a reputation... he is ‘that kind’ of biker. The one with a different girl in his bed every night. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/294a41ec-8d6a-4992-8afb-521094e3f685_zpsd3f77ac2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778028.jpg" alt=" photo 294a41ec-8d6a-4992-8afb-521094e3f685_zpsd3f77ac2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/52f471b8-4b64-443c-916f-f5d6ac041b8d_zpsda246015.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778029.jpg" alt=" photo 52f471b8-4b64-443c-916f-f5d6ac041b8d_zpsda246015.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now we fast forward three years... Tabby is 19 and in nursing school. Shy is no longer a recruit, but a member of Chaos. When Shy gets a call to check on Tab, he goes. Tab is out with some old friends from high school partying. Shy see’s how much potential Tab has, so he sets her straight. It doesn’t go over very smoothly. Tab is hurt and stays away from the MC for a while. Away from Shy. But she does get her act together. Graduates nursing school, becomes engaged to a nice normal guy. Then something big happens. Tab’s fiancée gets in an accident. Tabby is heart broken. Shy has always cared for Tabby, and even though she has ignored him for years, he wants to be there for her. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You need a safe place just to forget shit and escape, I’ll give it to you. Tonight. Tomorrow. Next week. Next month. That safe place is me, Tabby.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Shy and Tabby become ‘tight’. They spend a lot of time together and become very close friends. It was great to see their relationship change and grow. Tabby was doing better. Shy was helping her move on with her life, and letting her become the person she was always supposed to be. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Shy was giving me back me. He was guiding me to healing. </blockquote>
</b><br>Even though everyone warned Tabby about Shy (although they all like him, they know his reputation and Tabby has been through enough, they don’t want her hurt) Tab doesn’t care. She knows the real Shy. Although this quote was pretty funny...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m just tellin’ you to keep your eyes open and watch your heart. Or, more to the point, watch your ass because if you don’t, Shy’ll tap it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>There are some misunderstandings between the two of them (I wanted to slap Shy for a minute) but they get situated, and eventually, Shy and Tabby become a couple.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/4e12a79d-cdda-40df-84ab-3fafc7700948_zpsf47c7d77.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778030.jpg" alt=" photo 4e12a79d-cdda-40df-84ab-3fafc7700948_zpsf47c7d77.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I had a taste of you four years ago that I could never get off my tongue. Now, I've tasted more of you with more than just my mouth and I know I wanna keep it in a way I don't want to think of it bein' done. Not in a few weeks. Not in a few months. Maybe not ever"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br> They both are so in love with each other, but they keep it quite for a while because they are worried about others reactions- mainly, Tabby’s dad Tack. So they spend the next few weeks in love and happy. Shy’s brother Lan knows(loved Lan!) but everyone else was kept in the dark. Eventually, they are found out and things aren’t pretty. But in the end, it only brings them closer together as a couple. They always have each others backs and stick up for one another. NOTHING is more important to Shy than Tabby, not even his family of brothers in the MC. I love that about Shy. He proves time and time again how much he loves Tabby and how he has changed. He gets Tabby back to herself. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You promised to get me to a dream, you got me to a dream. Thank you, honey.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I love Tabby as a KA heroine. I loved her in MM and I loved her even more in this book. She is broken and trying to discover herself in the beginning, but she becomes strong and finds herself. I loved watching her grow from MM and from the beginning and end of this book. <br><br>Parker ‘Shy’ Cage... what to say about him... So hot and so freaking lovable. One word to describe him... <i>Swoon</i><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“May feel like you’re fallin’, Tabby, but remember, I’m at the bottom ready to catch you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Shy doesn’t just talk the talk, he walks the walk. He shows Tabby how much he loves her, and proves it to everyone time and time again. He stands up for her, is there for her, and will do anything to protect her<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Even beat the shit out of Dr. Dickhead. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Tabby and Shy face many obstacles. Both have had their fair share of tragedy. Their relationship isn’t an easy ride. But they find something in each other that both desperately need. Of course its a little emotional at times, and there is some drama (it wouldn’t be a KA book if there wasn’t) but their story was beautiful. I loved how their relationship spanned over the years. They went from not speaking, becoming best friends, and then lovers. This will definitely hold a spot in my top 3 favorite KA books. The epilogue was KA perfection. Can’t wait to read the rest of this series about Chaos and hopefully get much more Shy and Tabby!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m tellin’ you now, I want a lifetime.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/abaafe9d-85b6-443b-9f0e-85d9a3cd65ac_zps75b1928c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401126i/778031.jpg" alt=" photo abaafe9d-85b6-443b-9f0e-85d9a3cd65ac_zps75b1928c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer977558436885230047"><b>Oh. My. Gawd. I DREAMED AN EFFIN' DREAM AND IT IS THIS BOOK.</b> <br/><br/>Seriously, heaven in print. I thought there was no absolute way that this book could ever meet my ridiculously high, completely unreasonable expectations, but it did. In fact, it blew them out of the water.<br/><br/>Kristen Ashley takes us back to the badass world of Chaos and boy does she bring it. Shy is straight <i> gorgeous </i> and Tabitha is just adorable. I loved how Ashley depicted the evolution of their relationship and made this book totally </span>
  <span id="freeText977558436885230047" style="display:none"><b>Oh. My. Gawd. I DREAMED AN EFFIN' DREAM AND IT IS THIS BOOK.</b> <br /><br />Seriously, heaven in print. I thought there was no absolute way that this book could ever meet my ridiculously high, completely unreasonable expectations, but it did. In fact, it blew them out of the water.<br /><br />Kristen Ashley takes us back to the badass world of Chaos and boy does she bring it. Shy is straight <i> gorgeous </i> and Tabitha is just adorable. I loved how Ashley depicted the evolution of their relationship and made this book totally theirs while still giving us a sprinkle of Tack/Tyra and Hop/Lanie. <br /><br />KA is seriously a master at creating awesome characters--especially my personal favorite--the alpha male. I just love Chaos and I'm so glad she has made it a series. The excerpt for Fire Inside left me seriously hurting for more. I can't wait until June! </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer2244184793685409918">I see a bunch of my Goodreads friends reading a series and I immediately want to be one of the "cool kids" and read it too.<br/>Then I end up like this:<br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925469.gif' alt='Palm Springs commercial photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tabby Allen is the daughter of the Chaos Motorcycle Club's leader. She has a troubled life as a teenager with wanting to go out and party, one of the "brothers" Shy is on rescue duty aka Tabby Callout. He goes to the party and "takes" Tabby and brings her back to the club and offers for her to join the two naked women in his bed. He is of course t</span>
  <span id="freeText2244184793685409918" style="display:none">I see a bunch of my Goodreads friends reading a series and I immediately want to be one of the "cool kids" and read it too.<br>Then I end up like this:<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925469.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tabby Allen is the daughter of the Chaos Motorcycle Club's leader. She has a troubled life as a teenager with wanting to go out and party, one of the "brothers" Shy is on rescue duty aka Tabby Callout. He goes to the party and "takes" Tabby and brings her back to the club and offers for her to join the two naked women in his bed. He is of course trying to "scare her straight".<br><br>Later Tabby gets engaged and is actually happy. Tragedy strikes and now Shy steps in to help make everything all better.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925470.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Did you feel the sarcasm in that gif? You should.<br><br>Tabby has educated herself and tried to rise above the Club's motto's, she is working as a nurse and has her own place...but she might should just change her name to Doormat.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446909240i/16925471.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Her bestie even tries to give her some advice.<br><b>"He's a dawg, Tabby, and you can't forget that. If he's being cool with you, awesome. Pleased he's givin' that to you. Take it. You need family. I'm just tellin' you to keep your eyes open and watch your heart. Or, more to the point, watch your ass because if you don't. Shy'll tap it."</b><br>Tabby rolls her eyes to that advice.<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925472.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then this is the passage where I said to heck with this. I'm outta here:<br><b>He leaned slightly toward me and it took a lot not to lean back. "Is your phone broke?" he repeated, his voice back to low and menacing.<br>"No," I admitted.<br>"So, explain, if you're not avoiding me, you got a call from me, why don't you take it? And, Tab, I'll throw this out there now so you have plenty of time to come up with another excuse, when I leave a message, I wanna know why it isn't returned."<br>I stared at him and he stared at me.<br>I licked my upper lip, his eyes dropped to my mouth, his face got hard, and suddenly the room felt like a silent thunderclap rolled through it.<br>It was then I knew I couldn't take it anymore.<br>"I know about her," I whispered, and yes, that came right out, and yes, it sounded like an accusation.<br>"Say again?" he asked.<br>"I know about her. Your woman."<br>His brows went up. "So?"<br>So?<br>So?<br>"So, you didn't tell me about her," I pointed out.<br>"Sorry, Tab, didn't know I needed to report to you about who I fuck," he fired back.</b><br><br>It's totally a real love connection.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909538ra/16925500.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is something else that bugged the crap out of me.<br>The frigging obsession with her tongue.<br>This girl licks her lips and rolls that tongue out more than my dog does when he is licking his non-existent balls.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925473.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That just is so sexy. <br> <a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925474.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now get in line:<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446909240ra/16925475.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Booksource: library</i><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446909240i/16925476.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For the spotlight on this book I'm spotlighting my friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/506542650?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Brandie's review</a> I love her review and I totally trust Brandie's opinion. So I probably did read this one wrong. Brandie and I have been friends since I think about the first week I joined GR. I adore the girl, so go show her some love. </span>

<div id="review_562113326" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/562113326" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/562113326?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer562113326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16730957462045071179"><br/>Every new Kristen Ashley title is her <i>most anticipated book yet.</i> But somehow I think <i>Own the Wind</i> really is. Because in her own words <i>Own the Wind</i> is her <i>"first book with a bona fide publisher."</i><br/><br/>Tabitha (Tabby) Allen, nineteen year-old daughter of Chaos Club President, Kane "Tack" Allen has been getting into trouble for three years. Deciding it's best to keep Tabby's wild life from her father, members of the club take it on themselves to keep an eye on her and bring her home when necessary. These</span>
  <span id="freeText16730957462045071179" style="display:none"><br />Every new Kristen Ashley title is her <i>most anticipated book yet.</i> But somehow I think <i>Own the Wind</i> really is. Because in her own words <i>Own the Wind</i> is her <i>"first book with a bona fide publisher."</i><br /><br />Tabitha (Tabby) Allen, nineteen year-old daughter of Chaos Club President, Kane "Tack" Allen has been getting into trouble for three years. Deciding it's best to keep Tabby's wild life from her father, members of the club take it on themselves to keep an eye on her and bring her home when necessary. These 'Tabby Callouts' are discreet, under the radar hidden from Tack.<br /><br />Parker "Shy" Cage at twenty-four has had enough of 'Tabby Callouts' and decides to tame her wild side and teach her a lesson. Unfortunately Shy is wrong about Tabby, and his lesson hurts Tabby deeply.<br /><br /><br /><b>The Short Review:</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>For the Kristen Ashley Fans</i>
</b><br />You'll love it. Despite the shorter length and professional editing it still reads exactly like a Kristen Ashley novel.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>For the Kristen Ashley Virgins</i>
</b><br />This is a good title to start with as you'll get to read a well-edited version of a Kristen Ashley novel that is also a lot shorter than her self-published books.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>For those who enjoy Kristen Ashley but who want an edited story</i>
</b><br />You will notice and appreciate the difference in this first book with professional editors. My reservation here is that while the <i>editing</i> is very good, this is not the best <i>story</i> of hers that I've read. But still worth reading.<br /><br /><br /><b>The Long Review:</b><br /><br /><b>Writing Style</b> <br />Written in a similar style to most of Ms Ashley's books<br />...<i>One month later...</i>...<br />it starts out in the Prologue and Chapter One in third person, changing to first person (from Tabby's pov) from Chapter Two. There are also some short passages now and then in third person through Shy and Tack's eyes.<br /><br />It does contain some signature Kristen Ashley phrases.<br /><br /><b>Main Characters</b><br />Both Shy and Tabby are extremely likable characters. It's nice to see a short, curvy brunette as a heroine. Tabby is sweet but not silly, and though she’s had a hard time growing up with her real mother, she has been under the good influence of Tyra (her stepmother) for three years. She's loved Shy since she was sixteen, and is now studying to be a nurse. <br /><br />Shy is <i>not</i> shy. He's been with the Chaos Motorcycle Club since he was nineteen. Losing his parents when young, he and his brother have grown up in a harsh and unloving environment with their aunt and uncle. Now he works for the club. He's your typical Kristen Ashley alpha hero, but not obnoxious.<br /><br /><b>Other Characters</b><br />We see a fair bit of Tack and Tyra. Also introduced is Landon, Shy's brother. We also get a few brief appearances of previous characters associated with the Club or Tack. It's no secret that the H/h of book #2 <i>Fire Inside</i> are Hop and Lanie, and a bit of time is given over to them.<br /><br /><b>Time Line</b><br />The story opens when Tabby is nineteen and Shy twenty-four, although they have known each other since she was sixteen and he was twenty-one. Their story takes place over the next three years with the bulk of events happening when Tabby is twenty-two and Shy twenty-seven.<br /><br /><b>Editing</b><br />The editors have done a fine job of reducing the word count, eliminating the long, rambling sentences and excessive minutiae pertaining to clothes, accessories, etc and yet still keeping that distinctive tone of Kristen Ashley's writing that so many fans love. <br /><br />The story revolves around the Chaos Motorcycle Club and as such there is a degree of swearing. This is to be expected to maintain realism. But thankfully the amount of excessive and unnecessary cussing and profanity has been greatly reduced. <br /><br /><b>Sexist Language: A Warning</b><br />If you don't like sexist lingo <i>Own the Wind</i> may not be for you.<br />Where all the men are <i>brothers,</i> the women are referred to as <i>bitches</i> or <i>old ladies.</i><br /><br /><b>My Thoughts</b><br />Ratings and reviews are incredibly subjective. Almost every early reviewer has given <i>Own the Wind</i> 5 stars and an almost universal endorsement that this is Kristen Ashley's best book to date.<br /><br />It <i>is</i> a very good story. Undoubtedly for a reader who appreciates a polished and professionally edited story, this earns top marks. And importantly for the fans, it does retain Ms Ashley's unique story-telling voice.<br /><br /><i>Own the Wind</i> is good, but in my opinion it is not outstanding. (That honour would still go to <i>Sweet Dreams.</i>) What is outstanding is the quality of the editing that has allowed a Kristen Ashley story to still shine through despite the restrictions of a shorter word count.<br /><br />Whether the editors and Ms Ashley were trying to be too careful in this first outing together as a new couple, or they wanted to stick with a formula that works, there does seem to be quite a deal of restraint. Though it certainly ticks all the boxes, it lacks some of the emotional pull, intensity and inspiration of many of her previous works.<br /><br />The plot was not as compelling as some of her reads and I got the feeling that I'd read this before. Possibly the biggest letdown for me was her Epilogue. If there is one thing that Kristen Ashley never fails to produce is a spellbinding Epilogue that can almost be considered a book within a book they're usually that long. And satisfying. At 90% I hit the Epilogue and was looking for the pièce de résistance, all 10% of it. Unfortunately it went for only 2%, or 9 Kindle pages. And it was pretty average.<br /><br />Since first reading <i>Sweet Dreams</i> I've considered Kristen Ashley a great <i>story-teller.</i> The marriage with Grand Central Publishing has fine-tuned a raw talent into an accomplished <i>writer.</i> I hope this partnership continues.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 3<br /><br /><i>ARC courtesy of Grand Central Publishing via NetGalley</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16730957462045071179" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461287894" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer139678525146436039"><b>5 KA DeliciousDreams&BadassLove Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398450ra/770102.gif' width='400' height='176' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>- Hey mommy, <b>I dreamed a dream</b>, last night.<br/>-Aw, honey… Did you get scared?<br/>-No, mom it wasn’t like that. I saw that beautiful man again.<br/>-Pumpkin, men aren’t beautiful. They are called HANDSOME. Do you remember, how we talked about that and we said that boys are a little sensitive that way?<br/>-Yeah, mom, but he WAS *stomp foot*!!!! And he was shiny and and hadsome and beautiful and he comed to me riding.<br/>-It’s haNdsome, love and came, not comed. *sigh* So, riding? </i></span>
  <span id="freeText139678525146436039" style="display:none"><b>5 KA DeliciousDreams&amp;BadassLove Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398450ra/770102.gif" width="400" height="176" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>- Hey mommy, <b>I dreamed a dream</b>, last night.<br>-Aw, honey… Did you get scared?<br>-No, mom it wasn’t like that. I saw that beautiful man again.<br>-Pumpkin, men aren’t beautiful. They are called HANDSOME. Do you remember, how we talked about that and we said that boys are a little sensitive that way?<br>-Yeah, mom, but he WAS *stomp foot*!!!! And he was shiny and and hadsome and beautiful and he comed to me riding.<br>-It’s haNdsome, love and came, not comed. *sigh* So, riding? Hmmm… Did you see your prince on his white horse like Snow White?<br>-Nah…. Prince Charming is kinda lame, mom! <br><br>My man, came riding on his Harley, wearing his scuffed boots and his tight leathers. He took off his helmet and he put it on my head. When I grow up I will be his old lady and he will love me enough for 3 Princes, 2 Doctors and 5 Lawyers. Sorry, mom, but MY MAN, will fight my battles and he will love me forever, cussing and cursing, colouring my world, me always on the back of his motorcycle.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395955ra/762926.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <blockquote>
  <pre>TEAM BIKERS &amp; CHAOS CLUB</pre>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <i>Biker meets Biker Babe from birth</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770103.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Tabitha Allen</b> was born a Biker Princess. The daughter of Chaos Motorcycle Club's President, she always knew that the brothers got her back. She was born to ride. And she had the biggest crush on one of her father's "brothers". Until a fateful night, that by saving her, he broke heart and crashed her dreams. She moved on, the only way she knew, finding love and a future.<br><br><b>Parker "Shy" Cage</b> knows how much it hurts to lose family. So he protects his new one, the Club and its people, at every cost.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770104.jpg" width="400" height="243" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He lost Tabby before even getting her and just a taste years ago, haunts him. He understands that he doesn't stand chance and now he has to live with this mistake, trying to make the best out of his life. Find someone to ease his pain.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770105.png" width="400" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Life, tragedy and their deep feelings are bringing them back together, stronger, brighter and forever.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Always and forever, baby, you’re stuck with me.”</i>
</b><br><br>To dream again, to breath deep, to BE, they have to prove themselves to each other, their family, the Club and fate. Will fate be in their side, this time? Will they ride together? Or to earn this right, they will be asked to forfeit another?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770106.jpg" width="400" height="530" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Amazing and kickass, beautiful and awesome, in a way that only Kristen Ashley can deliver, this is a book about badasses and their women, another way of life, dangerous and liberating in an outlaw(-ish) kinda way. <br><br>Young but mature beyond their years, Shy and Tabby are growing up and falling deeper and deeper right in front of our eyes and we are witnessing their journey till they find each other. Life dealt them a hand and they are making the most of it, until the all in and them leaving with the pot. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770107._SY540_.png" width="400" height="557" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What makes this story even more beautiful and swoonworthy is the sheer amount of testosterone you experience.... Holy hotness, I wanted to rub my face in it!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391734ra/754278.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>SPECIAL GUEST STARS</b><br><b>Kane "Tack" Allen</b><br>Oh come on... A brother with a slutty past is messing with his daughter. What are you expecting??? I have to say, at first:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398450i/770108.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>but after some much needed epiphany:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/483325.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Lee Nightingale<br><br><i>you’re hiring Lee Nightingale and, girl, you know, that dude has had books written about him. They were fictionalized, but he’s also in the paper all the time, so we both know whoever wrote that shit did not tone it down. He’s the badass to end all badasses. He’s such a badass, he’s the freakin’ definition of badass, and his team of badasses only exist to define alternate nuances of the same thing.” Her chin jerked out. “Badass.”</i></b><br><br><b>Hawk Delgado<br><br><i>I also knew Hawk Delgado could totally join the cast of The Expendables but it was more likely he would act as a consultant on the film because Hawk Delgado didn’t playact badass. He just was one.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398450ra/770109.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>You don't mess with them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398451ra/770110.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>We also get a little insight in Hop's story that follows and without spoiling anything I'll only say that now I can't wait to read it. This book is missing the usual KA-bawl-your-eyes-out epilogue, but it makes sense because the "Chaos" series are more closely connected than her previous' ones. <br><br><b>KA fans you don't wanna miss this story!!! And you, yes I'm talking to you!! PICK A KA BOOK NOW!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398451ra/770111.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Bonus Quote courtesy of <b>Elvira</b>:<br><br><b>
  <i>If I was makin’ a porno, not that I’d make a porno, but, just sayin’, if I was, it’d be all about a UFC ring, sweaty hot guys with tape on their hands and shorts that come off easy, say, with that Velcro stuff at the sides. One yank and gone. You get what I’m sayin’?”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/368550.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>

<div id="review_509035150" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509035150" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509035150?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9781455599257" href="/book/show/17162785-own-the-wind">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=dirty-talk">dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=possessive-alpha">possessive-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=exceeded-my-expectations">exceeded-my-expectations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sea-world-misting-fan-worthy">sea-world-misting-fan-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=strong-willed-heroine">strong-willed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sweat-inducing">sweat-inducing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509035150" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18259148500528369249"><br/><b>5…10…15...20 Stars!! Absolute Perfection!! Shy and Tabby and <i>Own the Wind</i> embody everything that the Kristen Ashley name represents! She remained true to herself and her readers will NOT be disappointed. KA's brilliant story telling has been polished to a shine!! IT'S CLASSIC KA…GOLDEN!! </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I dreamed a dream"</i>
</b><br/><br/>I’m at a loss when I have to review a Kristen Ashley book. I sound like a broken record, because I say the same things over and over, but here I go again. Kristen Ashley is one of the few </span>
  <span id="freeText18259148500528369249" style="display:none"><br /><b>5…10…15...20 Stars!! Absolute Perfection!! Shy and Tabby and <i>Own the Wind</i> embody everything that the Kristen Ashley name represents! She remained true to herself and her readers will NOT be disappointed. KA's brilliant story telling has been polished to a shine!! IT'S CLASSIC KA…GOLDEN!! </b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I dreamed a dream"</i>
</b><br /><br />I’m at a loss when I have to review a Kristen Ashley book. I sound like a broken record, because I say the same things over and over, but here I go again. Kristen Ashley is one of the few authors that transports her readers into the story, you become a participant; a bystander watching it all play out, you are so close you can almost reach out and touch the characters. I <b>FEEL</b> so much when I’m reading one of her books, a whirlwind of emotions, it exhausts me and yet I am fulfilled, utterly content after I turn the last page, and <i>Own the Wind</i> was no exception!<br /><br />I loved Tabby’s sass, strength and determination. She’s grown since <i>Motorcycle Man</i> and continued to mature and become her own woman in <i>Own the Wind </i>. She doesn’t wait for life to come find her; she goes out and finds it herself. <br /><br />Shy is smart, and most of the time he’s logical and reasonable. He’s a bad boy for sure, and he’s described as a player by those who know him, but I don’t see him that way. Oh yeah, he’s got girls bouncing off his bed, but he’s up front on what he’s doing, honest about what he’s looking for, and doesn’t pit one chick against the other. I see him as a man with a really strong libido, and if woman are willing to fall into bed with him, who is he to say no!! He’s had some hard knocks in his life and when the beauty that is Tabby is willing to give him a shot, he grabs at it with everything that he is.<br /><br />Once they commit…nothing can come between them…another strong point in the story. Oh they fight, but they don’t waver! When these two get between the sheets, in the shower, on the counter...wherever...it is <b>EXPLOSIVE!!!</b> The heat is on and it does not stop! But what I loved the most, was their intimate conversations, where they come to terms with one another. Talk about their past and their future...<b>beautiful</b>! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Now I’m an us again, and that’s what I’ll be with my woman and the family we make until the day I fucking die."</i>
</b><br /><br />KA says some of the most profound things and relays powerful messages within the story. I love how the importance of family played into this book, all kinds of family…blood ties and also the club. Family is everything and you do whatever it takes to keep it together, but nothing comes between the one you’ve chosen to spend your life with. <br /><br />She also rocked the dialogue!! There are some amazing verbal smack-downs, like nothing I’ve ever read in any of her other books. It fires it off…bam bam bam …you can hardly keep up, it had me breathless, it was heartpounding, nailbiting, you are there in that moment…<b>fantastic!</b> <br /><br />So here are my final thoughts. In my opinion this is Kristen Ashley's most well rounded book, and the best she’s ever written. The story is a page turner, Tabby and Shy will capture your heart, and there is so much in the way of the other characters and setting that is familiar, it’s like going home. But most importantly, you will never doubt that the book you are reading is Kristen Ashley’s, her trademark storytelling is there is spades, yet it’s more defined, sharp, and has a professional stamp on it. Yes, the epilogue is not what we are used to, but it’s still <b>very good</b>, plus remember this is a continuing series, and just as we got to read about characters that are familiar to us in this book, I’m sure we will see Tabby and Shy’s story play out as the series moves forward. Last but not least, KA’s decision to partner with Grand Central Publishing was a smart move, as a businesswoman and most importantly as an author! I have no doubt that her fans will love this book as much as I did. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“May feel like you’re fallin’, Tabby, but remember, I’m at the bottom ready to catch you.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>Shy and Tabby’s song ~ <i>Count on Me</i> by Default</b><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=g1FQac3CqdQ">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=g1FQa...</a><br /><br />I know that life ain't always good to you.<br />I've seen exactly what it’s put you through<br />Thrown you around and turned you upside down and so you<br />You got to thinking there was no way out<br />You started sinking and it pulled you down<br />It may be tough you've to get back up<br />Because you know that life ain't over yet<br />I'm here for you so don't forget<br />You can count on me<br />Cause’ I will carry you till you <br />Carry on<br /><br />Anytime you need someone<br />Somebody strong to lean on<br />Well you can count on me<br />To hold you till the healing is done<br />And every time you fall apart<br />Well you can hide here in my arms<br />And you can count on me<br />To hold you till that feeling is gone…<br /><br /><br /><i>**ARC kindly provided to Swept Away By Romance courtesy of Grand Central Publishing, Kristen Ashley and Chas**</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="18259148500528369249" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1522641030" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1522641030" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1522641030?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=not-safe">not-safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=safe-with-exception">safe-with-exception</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=freebie-or-loan">freebie-or-loan</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=medical-personnel">medical-personnel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=mc">mc</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1522641030" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13946380223056471985"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 8/10/2016 and wrote following review)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4 Stars <i> (Re-Read* 6/12/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(2nd Re-Read** 10/6/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I liked this one. I really appreciated getting the H's POV more than usual, as it really helped me understand him. It also helped me feel and believe in their strong connection. It's no secret that I am a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> fan, so I'm not all that shocked that this was a winner for me. This had a lot of the typical KA features, but it also had difference</span>
  <span id="freeText13946380223056471985" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars <i>(Originally Read 8/10/2016 and wrote following review)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4 Stars <i> (Re-Read* 6/12/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 3.5 Stars <i>(2nd Re-Read** 10/6/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I liked this one. I really appreciated getting the H's POV more than usual, as it really helped me understand him. It also helped me feel and believe in their strong connection. It's no secret that I am a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> fan, so I'm not all that shocked that this was a winner for me. This had a lot of the typical KA features, but it also had differences (in a good way). I really liked this couple, and if it wasn't for the ending (see pacing below) I would've rated it higher :)<br /><br /><b>*Re-Read Update:</b> I enjoyed this again. I am going to keep my rating the same, as I felt pretty much the same as I did when I read it the first time. I'm still frustrated with the ending which prevented me from rating it higher, but an overall good re-read!<br /><br /><b>**Re-Read Update:</b> This was enjoyable, but just not quite as much as before. It very well could be the book funk I’m in, but the constant time jumps and half assed ending bugged me more this go-round. I still enjoyed the overall premise and the characters though. I’m just not sure if this will continue to be a re-read for me.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Tabby and Shy's story. Tabby is the mc's president's daughter and Shy is a brother, so when Shy gets called (yet again) to pick Tabby up from a party he isn't all that surprised. He lays it all out for her in a harsh way that her reckless behavior has got to stop, and he ends up hurting her. Shy didn't realize that he would lose her too, but he does and she avoids him for years because of his actions that one night. After a tragic event, he finds himself picking her up again and they start to form a friendship. The friendship turns into more, and they fall in love. There is some mc, family, and friend drama, some sweet moments, and some sexy times...and they do get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Tabby and Shy's POV. There seemed to be much more in the H's pov (as well as the h's) than there normally is in KA books. I liked that!<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good until the end. KA books always tend to be on the long side, so I was expecting that. What I didn't expect was that it seemed like an abrupt ending. Don't get me wrong -- I got my HEA...but it felt like it was missing that big conflict right before the ending that is so common in her books, and it really threw me off. I never skimmed and it flowed well otherwise.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They've known each other for years.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Shy. I liked him. He was the pushy alpha H that KA writes so well. I really appreciated how we experienced his regrets, and his longing for the h.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Tabby. I liked her, but I felt like she held on to her grudges too long at times.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I never needed any tissues, but I did shed a few tears.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H does something to snap the h out of her reckless behavior and ends up hurting her. She then avoids him for years and pushes even his friendship away. The H is the primary pursuer in the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some hot chemistry and scenes.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. Condoms are used until std testing and birth control happens. I don't remember any mention of the h's past practices, but the H says he had never gone without a condom.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h loses her fiancé and that is a large focus in their relationship as the H helps her heal. There is an OW that the H sees for 3 months (during their friendship because he didn't think the h would ever want more), and the h and H bump into her publicly once they're together.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There are 2 different chapters that start with the H waking up "in a pile of women". There is no descriptive sex with these women, but it is implied that things happened (both before anything happens with the h). There is also a scene with the H kissing his girlfriend (not sexual -- just kissing where the h sees).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>Not between mcs <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Thr H had some significant feelings for the h while with Ow, so it could be considered emotional cheating on the OW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Not really <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The beginning has them separate from being friends (with stronger feelings) to only bumping into each other for approximately 4 years -- but they weren't technically "together" for me to consider it an actual "separation". During this time, both have other partners (h gets engaged).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Manwhore H (off page), violence (pretty mild for mc romance - on and off page), h's loss of fiancé (on page through H's memories), murder of parents (H - off page), abusive caregivers (H - off page), and drug use by side character (off page). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b>This had good closure with a HEA ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[they get married <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I would've loved a farther jump ahead epilogue tbh -- but that is probably me just being greedy ;)<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it on loan through my local library.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd say that this is either <u>Safe with exception</u> or <u>Not Safe</u> for most readers depending on personal preferences.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating between mcs<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM (see above)<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H (see above)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does</b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_583463039" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/583463039" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/583463039?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer583463039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12674077577038590144">First off, I want to thank my friend Amanda for making it impossible for me to look at this cover title without thinking of flatulence. <br/><br/><b>2.5 stars.</b> Remember when I said I was on a long, long break from this author? I blame friends for dragging me back in. <br/><br/><i>Others :</i> Stacia, this one is EDITED. <br/><i>Me :</i> Nope. I'm not going there.<br/><i>Others :</i> But it's shorter. It's more polished. You know...<br/><i>Me :</i> Fine. I have at least 3 lives left. My curiosity is going to get me soon though.<br/><br/>I honestly think that the ship of </span>
  <span id="freeText12674077577038590144" style="display:none">First off, I want to thank my friend Amanda for making it impossible for me to look at this cover title without thinking of flatulence. <br /><br /><b>2.5 stars.</b> Remember when I said I was on a long, long break from this author? I blame friends for dragging me back in. <br /><br /><i>Others :</i> Stacia, this one is EDITED. <br /><i>Me :</i> Nope. I'm not going there.<br /><i>Others :</i> But it's shorter. It's more polished. You know...<br /><i>Me :</i> Fine. I have at least 3 lives left. My curiosity is going to get me soon though.<br /><br />I honestly think that the ship of 'hoping for something unique' has sailed for me. Ashley's got a formula and she's sticking to it. The hardcore fans love it and I get that. I just personally can't get excited about reading the same story over and over with only a few tweaks here and there. You can change the wrapping paper each time you re-gift, but there's still gonna be a Chia pet inside. <br /><br /><b>The Positive :</b> <br /><br />~ The editing and condensing helped. A LOT. I don't recall one 5 page scene of backyard BBQ details.<br />~ The characters were likable. Given that I don't generally like KA heroines, I was surprised to find that I liked Tabby. And Shy was more my speed than some of the super-roided out alphas I've seen before. I have a weakness for the tall and lean ones. <br />~ The steam content is always nice and the story was an easy read. For the first half, at least.<br /><br /><b>The Negative :</b><br /><br />~ There's nothing new to see here. The story is rearranged and the characters all still talk the same. And that remains the recurring problem (for me).<br />~ Shy put his hands on Tabby's mom by hitting her in the chest and pushing her into a wall. Not cool.<br />~ Like others have observed, it appears that the MC info was very poorly researched and/or lifted from television ideas. Nothing about that part of the story felt real.<br />~ The second half of the book had me skimming. I got bored after they got together and I didn't really care to want to read another "insert random scene of drama in the second half" again, so I skipped ahead a few chapters to the epilogue. <br /><br /><br />All in all, I wasn't impressed but I also didn't feel like I completely wasted a couple of hours. I enjoyed the sexy times and was able to breeze past some parts I didn't like. The editing is really what saved the book from being repetitive to the point of being bad. I know now that I'll probably never again read one of the older (pre-edited) <i>long</i> KA books, but I might at some point check out another one of the newer short books. <br /><br />My one big WTF moment (if you know me, you won't be suprised) : <i>It was more intoxicating than any liquor, a high better than any fucking drug.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12674077577038590144" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Turns out I kinda like these bad boy motorcycle a-holes . . . <br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/' rel='nofollow noopener'>

I now realize this whole biker scene is a vortex which is nearly impossible to pull yourself out of once you begin, but before I knew that I already had <i>Own the Wind</i> on hold at the liburrrrrrry (Kindle version only becau</span>
  <span id="freeText7892088889178484166" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>3.5 Stars<br><br>Hmmmmm.   <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455035366ra/18046459.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Okay. So even though this is the first in the series it’s really not because the Chaos Motorcycle Club was introduced in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1538647926?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcyle Man</a>. I now realize this whole biker scene is a vortex which is nearly impossible to pull yourself out of once you begin, but before I knew that I already had <i>Own the Wind</i> on hold at the liburrrrrrry (Kindle version only because ewwww - Holy Splooshfest, Batman). The reason???? The leading male was described as looking like this guy . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455035366ra/18046460.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yes please. Do want. <br><br>Alright, so like I said, even though this is book 1 it’s really more like book 2. The main characters are Tabby and Shy who were introduced back in <i>Motorcycle Man</i>. Tabby is the daughter of the Club’s President – Shy is one of the “brothers.” When we last saw Tab she was 16 – this book picks up a few years later. It was obvious she was creaming her underage jeans for Shy even back then, but since he was not interested in having a sitdown with Dateline he steered clear - and also because banging the Pres’ kid is strictly verboten. Long story short, <i>Own the Wind</i> does the fastforwardy timeline, bad shit happens, Tab and Shy play the will they/won’t they game for LIKE. FUCKING. EVER. and finally they get down to bidness. And unlike the Super Bowl halftime show, the smexytimes in this book were f-in’ . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455035366ra/18046461.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think my underwears melted.<br><br>Anyway, then more stuff happens and angst and drama llama and a bunch of totally not necessary monkeywrenches get thrown in, but luckily there was plenty more . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455035366ra/18046462.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>thrown in to keep my interest. <br><br>These books have zero nutritional value, but somehow I want to eat a whole cabinet full of them anyway. I have no excuse for myself. At this point I am claiming that I won’t be reading the entire series because <b>600+ PAGES FOR BOOKS 3 AND 4</b>?!?!?!?! Damn. Get thee to a book editor, Kristen Ashley. However, I would not place money on my ability to stay away. I also thought I’d have no interest in reading “Hop’s” book (which is the next in this series) after wanting to straight up pull a Cassius Clay on his ballsack, but then they talked about his mustache and it sounds very . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455035366i/18046463._SY540_.jpg" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So now I’m getting ready to immediately run back to the library website because . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455035366ra/18046464.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I need an intervention. <br><br>The one good thing to come out of this is proof that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1404624174?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Shelby</a> and I do not share one brain. She read this 100% wrong and now I’m not sure we can be friends any longer ; )</span>
  <a data-text-id="7892088889178484166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
