<div id="review_614998174" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/614998174" />
    <a title="Aly is so frigging bored" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored"><img alt="Aly is so frigging bored" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574767515p2/4290492.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614998174?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aly is so frigging bored" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aly is so frigging bored" href="/user/show/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored">Aly is so frigging bored</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lovers of neanderthals and Mary Sue heroines</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Aly is so frigging bored by: </span>
      Group reading
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored?shelf=wtf-was-i-thinking">wtf-was-i-thinking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored?shelf=never-ending-aka-never-finished">never-ending-aka-never-finished</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored?shelf=epic-fail">epic-fail</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614998174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13550073112718056302">To whoever added this to the group and proceeded to vote for it: I hate you and I'll send you poop for your birthday, till the end of time.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421522i/837401.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>It’s not me, it’s you book, all you!<br/><br/>This book made me so mad that I wanted to chuck my laptop out the window. I will never pick up a book by this author[side note: the female character from another of her books should have clued me in that this wasn’t for me, but it serves to see that I am a masochist; who the hell sleeps with a dude for over 6 months without</span>
  <span id="freeText13550073112718056302" style="display:none">To whoever added this to the group and proceeded to vote for it: I hate you and I'll send you poop for your birthday, till the end of time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421522i/837401.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It’s not me, it’s you book, all you!<br><br>This book made me so mad that I wanted to chuck my laptop out the window. I will never pick up a book by this author[side note: the female character from another of her books should have clued me in that this wasn’t for me, but it serves to see that I am a masochist; who the hell sleeps with a dude for over 6 months without knowing his name?!] or from this contemporary sub-genre.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/9fwvx6a" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421522i/837402.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I try never to do this since I respect authors a lot, but WHAT THE HELL Ms. Ashley? WHAT THE HELL? If you need synonyms use a frigging thesaurus not the same word over and over and over and over and over and over again! See how annoying that is, see?? Examples of great literature(and this only from 2 or 3 pages):<br><i>“Baby, bein’ your safe harbor doesn’t come with me gettin’ pissed when you gotta do what you gotta do when you gotta do it.</i><br><a href="http://imgur.com/8Ro8AVb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421522ra/837403.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>or<br><i>Jason hated my apartment. Not frequently but often enough to make his point, when we were cuddling on the couch watching TV or he was sitting on a stool at the bar watching me ruin dinner, he’d say something like, “Can’t wait until we can get you out of this pit.”<br>It wasn’t a pit. It was old and worn, but it wasn’t a pit.<br>Jason thought it was a pit.<br>Looking at Shy leaning into the counter, he didn’t look like he thought my place was a pit.</i> <br>Thank you for repeating it. I really enjoyed that. I did!<br><i>That sucks, huge, so huge it’s impossible to measure how huge that sucks, it’s that huge.</i><br>My last neuron... he just died from sadness. <br><br>It's like the characters are retarded: they repeat what other character said or repeat what they said/thought some moments ago. Are you all so dim?? Do you have a memory problem? Besides that I don't understand the thought patterns of any of these characters, they have so convoluted ways of considering problems and talking that I just couldn’t keep up.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/lHbqWDf" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421522ra/837404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Apart from this MAJOR problems, let me tell you about the characters… We have the death-to-feminism-and-other-diseases hero who is the perfect example of the ‘80s bodice reapers dudes. It’s obvious he hates women and disrespects them(the overuse of the word “bitch” gave him away) and, like in those novels, I presume he’ll come to see that HIS woman, not all the gender, are worthy of respect. Besides this dominant character flaw he can’t just make up his mind: he disrespects, talks down to and insults the heroine and then he wanders why she avoids his shitty ass, shame on her for doing it too!<br><a href="http://imgur.com/AM5iXeD" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421522ra/837405.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Now, the heroine… she is the washed out copy of a snarky heroine and to add to it, stupid as well. He reduces her to tears, literally, and after 2 years or so he’s the best thing from toilet paper! This Tabitha[every time I see the name I think of the amazing character from dark Hunters that this idiot doesn’t even come close to] is from the earthworm-brained, TSTL category: she can’t make up her mind, is a coward and shacks up with the king of the world from above.<br><br>Additionally the names from this books… I hate them. I don’t want to get into this since it will take me forever, but what the hell names are those?!<br><br><b>All in all, I came to the conclusion that this biker book, and maybe all the others, is the re-enactment of the 80s bodice rippers, but with crappy clothing, bad language, stupid people, lesser manners, an uglier setting and the “fuck you grammar, I hate you” attitude. And if we are really lucky, we might find drug dealers and arms dealers too! </b><br><br><br><br><i>All this was brought after 20% of reading, imagine what I could have done if I read more... I shudder in fear</i>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13550073112718056302" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

HELLS YEAH we all have SO MUCH to look forward too!!!<br /><br /><i>A HUGE THANK YOU to Netgalley and Grand Central Publishing for providing with an ARC to read and review - yes folks you read it right, this book is up on Netgalley... run, i say, RUN over there and request it if you have an account NOW!!!</i></b></span>

The concept was sound. Execution was lacking. I was excited about reading this as an ARC. I liked Motorcycle Man. But, have to say, if you've read that one, you've pretty muc</span>
  <span id="freeText6333550622205822390" style="display:none">03/28/2013 -- FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED --<br /><b><br />Overall Rating = 2.5 Stars<br />Book Cover / Book Blurb = 2 / 2 = 2 Stars<br />Writer’s Voice = 2.5 Stars<br />Character Development = 3 Stars<br />Story Appreciation = 2.5 Stars<br />Worth the Chili = 3 Stars [Was an ARC, $3.79 on Amazon]<br /></b><br />I think it is safe to say this isn't one of my favorite Kristen Ashley books. The concept was sound. Execution was lacking. I was excited about reading this as an ARC. I liked Motorcycle Man. But, have to say, if you've read that one, you've pretty much read this one. Nothing new...<br /><br /><b>A few things I liked:</b><br />1 – Shy and Tabby. They were actually pretty good characters, but here is the deal … they used much of the same dialogue I’ve seen in other characters created by this author. Their appearance is remarkably similar to other characters she has created. I liked them, but they were not unique in any form or fashion.<br /><br />2 – I didn’t note any editing issues, but these haven't been a hot button for me in the past. Even so, this one was more polished compared to the wrongly spelled, poorly used verbiage we've experienced in the past. We all know, if the story is good, you can overlook much. We still have the stilted dialogue and the run on sentences. These have been described as Kristen Ashley trademarks. I’m not buying it. When you stop and look at some of this dialogue it just sounds stupid. You expect the guy to start pounding his chest and UGG’ing. I know men of few words. They aren’t men of few words because they don’t know how to talk or don’t know how to be polite, they are men of few words because they choose their words and battles wisely. I know bikers and to equate bikers with the degree of intelligence you see displayed here is just not fair.<br /><br />3 – The cover informs the reader quickly about the subject content. I like knowing immediately about the contents. Does it pull me? Hmm… maybe a bit.<br /><br />4 – The story length. Some of my favorite books were written by this author once upon a long time ago. One of the things I really liked was the longer length of story. When I like a story, I don’t want it to end. I absolutely did not feel this way about this one. It was mediocre in its’ best moments and I couldn’t finish it fast enough.<br /><br /><b>Unfortunately, I found more to not like than like in this one – here are a few things:</b><br />1 – Where was the story?<br /><br />2 – Characters I’ve read in other books by this author over again. Almost like playing Barbies. We can change their hair color, change their clothes and maybe put them in a fairy castle instead of a cabana by the pool, but they are still the same Barbies. Nothing different or exciting. Therefore, not really worth the time.<br /><br />3 – The dialogue and run on sentences employed by this author are beyond annoying. They were at a minimum with this book, but were still present. Enough to annoy me.<br /><br />4 – Did anyone else notice the similarity to a “Sons of Anarchy” episode? A very strong resemblance. A few of the characters were almost identical. I love the show and think it is escape’ism at its best. I thought this book a mediocre to poor copy.<br /><br />5 -- A very noticed shortcut taken in writing this story surprised me. Maybe this was an effort to cut length. Not sure. At the beginning of almost every chapter you jump ahead; a week, two weeks, a day, three days. Almost every chapter. This is a shortcut transition style that I don't think works well - unless used sparingly. There is so much you feel you miss. You feel slighted. This is the cheap way out and it surprised me this author took that shortcut. I don't know about other readers, but for me, if this is an example of what happens when a writer finds a publisher, I'm not sure I think it is all worth it.<br /><br />I will to continue to give KA the benefit of the doubt for a bit longer. I will continue to hope for the best and prepare for the worst. I wouldn’t say this is my least favorite K. Ashley book, but it is leaps away from my favored Sweet Dreams [in the wrong direction]. I can hope … maybe next time? I'm sure at some point I'll give up trying.<br /><br />It didn’t happen for me this go ‘round. There are so many rave reviews for this one. I’m not one of them, but many felt this was a great offering. I hope when you read it, you feel the way they did. I wish I could :o|<br /><br />I hope you are happy reading this one.<br /><br /><i>ARC provided by the publisher and author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /><br />+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++<br />I said this in a comment to someone as I was reading this book. The more I thought about it, it summed up my thoughts pretty clearly:<br /><i>Just don't know anymore about this author. Same song, different verse ... like riding down the road with your iPod shuffle on repeat. Works until you get sick of it and then you won't ever listen to the song again, or, if you do -- "oh, yeah. I used to like that song, until ...". Know?</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="6333550622205822390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer461228955&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461228955" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6903455544761180474"><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/neilpatrickharrislickslips.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398442ra/770076.gif' alt=' photo neilpatrickharrislickslips.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Okay, let's just start off by saying that I rated this story a 4.5 star. The reason being, I was so excited, and eagerly anticipating a HUGE dangerous & dramatic scene at the end... and I didn't get one (or the one I was expecting (sorry!). <br/>I get what KA was doing.. any possible risk of losing Shy being the most devastating thing that Tabby would have to go through <i>again</i> being an enormous tragedy, but for me it just wasn't that... on the edge, chewing your nails, wondering what's going to ha</span>
  <span id="freeText6903455544761180474" style="display:none"><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/neilpatrickharrislickslips.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398442ra/770076.gif" alt=" photo neilpatrickharrislickslips.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Okay, let's just start off by saying that I rated this story a 4.5 star. The reason being, I was so excited, and eagerly anticipating a HUGE dangerous &amp; dramatic scene at the end... and I didn't get one (or the one I was expecting (sorry!). <br>I get what KA was doing.. any possible risk of losing Shy being the most devastating thing that Tabby would have to go through <i>again</i> being an enormous tragedy, but for me it just wasn't that... on the edge, chewing your nails, wondering what's going to happen next, a climax that I'm so used to in KA stories. <br><br><br>What I LOVED about this story was being able to <i>witness</i> Shy and Tabby growing up and maturing.<br><br>1) Tabby 19 years old - Shy 23: Tabby partying with her friends &amp; Shy over-reacting and ending up being a <i>dick</i> to her. He breaks her heart. <br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics/wordshurt-1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398442ra/770077.gif" alt=" photo wordshurt-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She gives him a kiss to let him know what he's missing out on (and he never forgets the taste of). Tabby then straightens up, focuses on her studies to become a nurse, and makes him invisible for a couple of years.<br><br>2) Tabby then on the street with her boyfriend, all dolled up and looking at him like there's no one else in the world around them. Shy sees them together and realizes that if he wants to have "that" then he better stop acting like a dawg.<br><br>3) Tabby's fiancé (Jason) is killed in a car accident, and Shy knows he can't go to her directly (because he's still invisible to Tabby) but helps her and supports behind the scenes.<br><br>4) After many months of mourning Jason's death, Tabby decides she needs a night out, so she goes out with her best friend since high-school, Nathalie. Nathalie never grew up and is still partying like crazy, except she's partying with a dangerous crowd. Tabby doesn't like the situation she's in and calls Shy because she doesn't want the club &amp; her father to find out about it.<br><br>5) Once Tabby lets Shy 'back in', they start to build a different kind of relationship. They become good friends. They hang out, cook dinner together, watch movies, and go for rides. They also begin to trust one another with stuff they never shared with anyone else.<br><br>6) Tabby goes to the compound one day, and sees Shy with another woman, and realizes he has an 'old lady'... and this almost kills her. She's upset, sad, and angry that Shy never told her he had a woman since she considered them really close. Shy calls her later on, and she freezes him out..again. After avoiding him for a couple of days, Shy is waiting for Tabby in her apartment when she gets home from work. She confronts him about 'Rosalie', and he loses his mind because he can't believe she's freezing him out since he listened to her talk about her dead fiancé while she was in deep mourning and didn't hold that against her. He leaves mad because now he doesn't want to have anything to do with her for a while. <br><br>7) After a month of not talking, Shy finds out that Tabby has taken a job across the country and is leaving soon. He freaks out, storms into her apartment and tells her she can't go... and then he kisses her..and she kisses him back. They both put all the feelings they've been holding into that kiss, and by the time they finish kissing, they're both breathless, and weak-kneed. Shy tells her she has 2 hours to get her shit sorted out, then she's to go to his apartment.<br>Tabby goes to Shy's apartment and they make love for the first time.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/shyandtab.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398442ra/770078.gif" alt=" photo shyandtab.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>“I have never, not once, not in my life, made love to any woman. Not once. Not until what I just did with you.” </i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/seth.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398442i/770079._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo seth.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tabby is scared and has a lot of questions about how their relationship is going to be, and because they have such an awesome foundation already in place, Shy knows exactly what Tabby worried about before she even has to voice it.<br><br>.... and this brings the reader to the most amazing place in the story. <br>We've been able to be apart of their character and relationship development, and now we're finally able to see them be 'on the same page' as each other in their lives. <br><br>This is what I like to call a 'divine point' in their lives. <br>They were <i>destined</i> to be together, but they had to go through all the other stuff first in order to reach this point. This is so they would be 'ready' for one another, and be prepared and equipped to take the next step that will shape their lives. It is because they've been through all the other stuff that they're able to stand together (strong) when they are attacked, and ridiculed by the people they know and love.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/shyandtabby.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398442i/770080._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo shyandtabby.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is where the 'adventure &amp; trouble' part of the story begins.<br><br>I really enjoyed this story, and I LOVED seeing Elvira, 'Hawk", Lee, Brock, and Mitch *sigh*. <br><br>... and the ending &amp; epilogue <b>
  <i>BEAUTIFUL!</i>
</b><br><br><br><br>If your a fan of Bad-ass-biker dudes &amp; and kick-ass, smart &amp; sassy women - THEN READ THIS BOOK!!<br><br><br><b>Favorite quotes:</b><br><br><i> "I'm alive. You're alive. I gotta work to live so I do that and I'll have to do that for a long lime. But when I'm not workin', I'm livin'. So let's ride." <br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/albums/i477/hebbies37/review%20pics/?action=view&amp;current=chaos1.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398442i/770075.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>"I dreamed a dream, Shy Cage."<br>He shifted so his hips were against mine and his voice was now raw when he ordered, "Shut up, baby, and kiss me."<br>"I dreamed a dream when I was sixteen and here I am, standing with my dream, feeling it come real."<br>"Fuck me," he muttered.<br>Then I knew he'd lost patience because Shy slanted his head and kissed me.<br>Yes.<br>I dreamed a dream and there I was, a ring on my finger, my man's mouth on mine, standing with my dream, feeling it come real.<br>I was feeling everything.<br>And it was beautiful."<br><br>"So Shy lowered his voice and reminded him, "She's not your little girl anymore, not like that. She may always be your, little girl in some ways, brother, but not like that. You gave me the chance, I would have told you, this is solid. We started out and it was friends. That wasn't what I wanted, it was what she needed, so I gave it to her. We built on that. The foundation is laid and it's the kind that holds fast. This is it, brother. We're livin' together. Soon's we can do it, we're movin' to a better fuckin' place so I can provide her with a decent home. I'm puttin' my ring on her finger, I'm givin' her babies, and when she's laid to rest, that ring I give her will still be on her finger. I see you're accepting this now, so you need it all and there it is. I was a part of an us and I was happy. Some motherfucker killed my parents and took that from me, so life forced me to become nothin' but me. Now I'm an us again, and that's what I'll be with my woman and the family we make until the fucking day I die."<br>"Christ, Shy," Tack whispered.<br>"I think now you totally fuckin' feel me." </i><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["The best part of the ceremony was after Shy kissed his bride, and when we were done, he didn't let go. So I stood in his arms, my thumb stroking his jaw, my eyes gazing up at him. the world had melted away, so I didn't hear the hoots and hollers of friends and family.<br>I only heard what he muttered in a voice that was weirdly raw but unbelievable beautiful: "Like I'm the only man on the planet."<br>In that minute, he was but then again, for me, really, when it came down to it, he always had been." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/kiss3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398442i/770081.jpg" alt=" photo kiss3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer581905688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8823964666595022126">**2.5 stars**<br/><br/><b>At last!! I finished!! Three days of reading this book are finally over! **Happy dance!**</b><br/><br/>Now for my review. It is safe to say that I am not a Kristen Ashley fan-girl. I have read one other book by her before this, which I enjoyed, so I was hopeful for this one. However, this book definitely falls in the "negatives outweigh the positives" category. By the end of this book I was just praying for it to be over. Let's start with some good news, shall we?<br/><br/>What I liked:<br/>1) <i>The beginning.</i> I </span>
  <span id="freeText8823964666595022126" style="display:none">**2.5 stars**<br /><br /><b>At last!! I finished!! Three days of reading this book are finally over! **Happy dance!**</b><br /><br />Now for my review. It is safe to say that I am not a Kristen Ashley fan-girl. I have read one other book by her before this, which I enjoyed, so I was hopeful for this one. However, this book definitely falls in the "negatives outweigh the positives" category. By the end of this book I was just praying for it to be over. Let's start with some good news, shall we?<br /><br />What I liked:<br />1) <i>The beginning.</i> I didn't mind the time jumps and I was excited to see some backstory about Tabby and Shy's relationship. <br /><br />2) <i> The sex.</i> Kristen Ashley SURE knows how to write a hot love scene! I think she has the panty-dropping scenes down to a science. <br /><br />What I hated:<br />1) <i>Shy himself.</i> Ugh, I wanted to slap Shy so badly for the entire second 1/2 of the book. He is so freaking arrogant and controlling. Don't get me wrong, I like an alpha male as much as the next girl but when a man tells me <i>"... you can get pissed, you can rant, you can try sweet, I am not washin' clothes and I'm not pushin' a vacuum. Do you understand me?",</i> I would be SHAKING with anger. No I don't understand you, buddy! You don't have to want to vacuum but I would certainly expect a discussion about it, not just a "I ain't doing that, you feel me?"!!! No way, Jose! That isn't how a relationship works. Want another example of something he said that made me FUMING mad? <i>"You nag or bust my balls, I can dump my clothes wherever the fuck I want at my place or the Compound, and I won't have a woman gettin' up in my face about it."</i> Mind you, these conversations were after the two were in a serious, committed relationship. You just don't talk to your partner like that, you just don't. What made me knock down stars left and right was that <i>I didn't want to be Tabby or envy Tabby in her relationship with Shy. I was so HAPPY that my husband is nothing like him!</i> That isn't what you want from your alpha hero. <br /><br />2) <i> Tabby herself.</i> She was doormat central in this relationship. She talks a big talk about how she is going to balance him and not let him walk all over her but each time he argues with her, she says, "He was right." It is like a freaking annoying broken record. <br /><br />3) <i> The situation with Tabby's boss at work.</i> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I would FLIP OUT and file a restraining order if my boyfriend went behind my back and beat the crap out of my boss. In no way is that hot or sexy or him taking care of her. That is INSANE. If she was getting abused or she was getting beaten and Shy walked in and saved the day, sure, kick the crap out of that guy. But if a doctor is harassing you, a nurse, at work, your boyfriend beating the ever living shit out of him behind your back is just crazy-town.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />4) <i>Kristen Ashley's writing.</i> Now I'm really going to get the fans rallying against me. I felt like this book had...well... no point. It was just a rambling series of mundane events in the life of a couple. Sure, there were things that happened, but it didn't feel like this story had a beginning, a middle, and an end. I also spend 4 pages reading an argument about whether or not to buy a refrigerator that makes crushed ice... **crickets**. Also, I couldn't stand the way that all of her characters spoke in truncated sentences. What is their beef with pronouns?! They are there for a reason! <br /><br />Surprisingly, I find myself wanting to move on to the next book in the series. I have the ARC already so I'm going to give it a try. I hope it is an improvement on this one for my tastes. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8823964666595022126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

I mean, I</span>
  <span id="freeText4201905745069381580" style="display:none">I dreamed a dream in time gone by<br>When hope was high and life worth living<br>I dreamed that love would never die<br>I dreamed that God would be forgiving<br><br>Then I was young and unafraid<br>And dreams were made and used and wasted<br>There was no ransom to be paid<br>No song unsung, no wine untasted ..<br><br>“You shittin’ me, are you fuckin’ shittin me, Mo, you think this was as good as Sweet fuckin’ Dreams”….. “Well, maybe not as good as but I am on a bit of a high here at the moment after reading about Shy Cage….. I mean, I do love you Tate, you know I do, but seriously do you not think that Shy is some real badass piece of shit…. I mean, if you were gay….. oK, me Bad, would you not turn for him?” “Fuck No, Mo, you mean the world to me – those other bithches meant nothing to me – that Baba, she has my name tattooed on her profile on Goodreads but she means nothing to me, she knows that you found me first and I am yours. Hell, she can’t even decide who she wants she has so many names tattooed on her. So I ain’t too happy that you think that Shy Cage is a badass biker that you could do – hey, ain’t he too fuckin’ young for you – he is only 27 – Jesus, Babe, you are old enough to be his fuckin’ mother”… “Nice one Tate, way to go to get a BJ tonight. All I am saying is that if anything ever happened between us, I could seriously go for Shy…. “<br><br>Sorry, girls…. Was away in my own little Denver world there for a while…. Yep, I found someone who could rival my one true love, Mr Tatum Jackson. Shy Cage…. A fuckin’ Dawg of the highest order – screws multiple women at a time, couldn’t give a shit about his reputation BUT he has his own One True Love – Tabby, Tabitha, Tab. Tabitha Allen, beautiful daughter of the equally beautiful Tack Allen and step-daugher of Ty-Ty.<br><br>This was great – won’t go into to much detail about the story line as it has been done before but would like to said that I was a little disappointed with Ms KA’s last book Raid. Wondered if she was going to desert her fans now that she had got the magic publishing deal. I mean there was a time when I would email her and she would reply but not any more. I don’t begrudge her her fame. She deserves it. But after Raid I thought, No, Kristen, stay true to form. So it was with a bit of trepidation that I embarked on the story of Shy and Tabby. I was NOT disappointed. It had all the elements that I loved from some of her previous books. The clothes descriptions, shoes, belts, earrings. The room descriptions, duvets, pillows, photoframes…… Sigh, Shy – you sweet, sweet boy. .. LOVED IT. Off to bed soon to DREAM about Shy. Tate, you keep your hands to yourself tonight…. And Elvira, she deserves a special mention. She was great. And the next book sounds like it will be fan fuckin’ tastic. <br>What to read next?     <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1449581089" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer996766146114545597"><b>Amazon Kindle Daily Deal 25Jul18 <a href='https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00AMIL9C8/ref=s9_acsd_hps_bw_c_x_7_w?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&pf_rd_r=S8KGMRGX86GA9DGMC75Z&pf_rd_r=S8KGMRGX86GA9DGMC75Z&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=232ccc1a-905e-48b4-95fd-5cd8348007c1&pf_rd_p=232ccc1a-905e-48b4-95fd-5cd8348007c1&pf_rd_i=11552285011' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a> $1.99</b><br/><br/>I ♥♥♥ Kristen Ashley but she isn't for everyone. Still I enjoyed this book overall.<br/><br/><b>3.5 I Dreamed a Dream Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Have you read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_' title='Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Motorcycle Man</a>?</b> If the answer is no…STOP now. Do not pass go, do not collect two-hundred dollars because even though this says Chaos #1 I think your enjoyment will be dramatically reduced without that foundation. At least for me Shy would have had an unsurmountable deficit to overcome if I hadn’t spent time in the Chaos compound an</span>
  <span id="freeText996766146114545597" style="display:none"><b>Amazon Kindle Daily Deal 25Jul18 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00AMIL9C8/ref=s9_acsd_hps_bw_c_x_7_w?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&amp;pf_rd_r=S8KGMRGX86GA9DGMC75Z&amp;pf_rd_r=S8KGMRGX86GA9DGMC75Z&amp;pf_rd_t=101&amp;pf_rd_p=232ccc1a-905e-48b4-95fd-5cd8348007c1&amp;pf_rd_p=232ccc1a-905e-48b4-95fd-5cd8348007c1&amp;pf_rd_i=11552285011" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a> $1.99</b><br><br>I ♥♥♥ Kristen Ashley but she isn't for everyone. Still I enjoyed this book overall.<br><br><b>3.5 I Dreamed a Dream Stars</b><br><br><b>Have you read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a>?</b> If the answer is no…STOP now. Do not pass go, do not collect two-hundred dollars because even though this says Chaos #1 I think your enjoyment will be dramatically reduced without that foundation. At least for me Shy would have had an unsurmountable deficit to overcome if I hadn’t spent time in the Chaos compound and had a little history going into this. <br><br><b>Shy</b><br><br>Let’s say that Shy <b>IS</b> a D. O. double Gee, that spells DOGG. He apparently takes women whose names he can’t remember to bed, often more than one at a time and when we first get a glimpse of him here he is asleep under a few Chaos hoochies when he gets called out to go reel in Tabby and get her home. Shy thinks maybe she needs a lesson one only he can teach her.<br><blockquote>
  <i> Hopefully, in about two seconds, she’d be a lot more than kinda freaked out. <b>She’d be scared straight and out of this bullshit she kept pulling.</b> Therefore, two seconds later, he yanked her into his room, tugged her to a stop and flipped the light switch. The two women were still naked, lying head to foot on the bed, having, since he was gone, tangled with each other. Briefly, he tried to remember their names.</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448917013i/17205873._SX540_.png" width="400" height="215" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You think he’d stop there but nope….<br><blockquote>
  <i>“But you… you made assumptions. You showed you decided exactly the kind of girl I was that night when that guy took his hand to me without knowing one single thing about me. I wasn’t what you thought, Shy. <b>I didn’t need your shit and I also didn’t deserve it. Family doesn’t make judgments. They talk. They support.</b> You made a judgment. You acted on that judgment. You doing it hurt me so that means you are not my family.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385998247ra/7271269.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And even after he has seen some stuff and realized that he has never felt anything for anyone like Tabby felt for the man she lost when he gets her call late at night for some help…<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Get her ass up. Both of you need to get dressed and get gone.” He reached into the nightstand and grabbed his gun, shoving it into the back waistband of his jeans and pulling his tee over it. “You got fifteen minutes to get out. You’re not gone by the time I get back, I will not be happy.” <br>“Sure thing, babe,”</i>
</blockquote><br>Who are these hoochies that are happy to have threesomes with a guy that throws them out right after???<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406814834ra/10601858.gif" width="400" height="229" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And at this point I’m thinking <i>Shy you are a complete douchecanoe and I’m not sure I’m ever going to like you.</i> <b>It is a pretty big hole even for KA to dig an alpha out of. But she did it!!!</b><br><br>Thank goodness that most of the OTT jerkface things happen in the first 15% but still I’m not one to be gung ho for a leading man that can’t even remember the names of the women he is sleeping with. Still what it comes down to is that KA makes me believe that Shy was miserable in the life he had before Tabby and she was his wake up call he just never thought he’d deserve her.<br><br><b>Tabby</b> <br><br>Tack’s only little girl grew up a Chaos princess. She has been around the hard life of the brothers for most of her life and she knows what happens with some of the brotherhood. She fell in love with a man outside that life and was ready to give him everything until a tragedy stuck and she lost her man and her dream. Shy was there for her in a way no one else could be and he brought her back from that depression and the hole that was left in her heart.<br><br>However when she falls for Shy, the notorious hound dog, it leads to one of the best Adult to Child coming of age blow-outs I’ve ever read. Tack and Tyra are an alpha couple all the way so it took some doing for Tabby to show them she isn’t a little girl anymore and I LOVED the entire thing. Seriously this book was worth reading just for that conversation between Tabby and Tyra and then Tabby and Tack. She is a strong woman who will not be told who she can or can’t fall in love with and I totally love that about her.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“You know you’re Dad’s one-and-only, Tyra, and if you don’t know this, seeing as he had kids before he met you, I’m sorry to tell you but even though you’re his one-and-only now, you weren’t his one-and-only.”<br>Her head jerked, she flinched, and I finally saw it. Understanding. <br>“You feel me,” I said softy. “I get I’m not Shy’s one-and-only but I still… fucking… am.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Go Tabby you stand up for your man.<br><br><b>Shy and Tabby</b><br><br>This is really more of a love story than most of KA’s books. There is some building tension with a new player in the drug game that is trying to get into Chaos territory and some trouble with one of Tabby’s no good friends from high school but for the most part this is just a story about Tabby and Shy finding their way to one another and learning how to accept the other for who they are.<br><br>The biggest confrontation is when Tabby and Shy are found out and there are repercussions with the members of Chaos. Shy did some stuff in this that totally redeemed him with me.<br><br>❶ - He apologized for some of the things he said to Tabby when she was younger and for treating her like he did when he judged her and thought he was helping.<br><br>❷ - Shy totally stood up for Tabby and even though some of the boys think it is cool to boss their old ladies around, Shy doesn’t play like that.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Tab and I don’t play it that way. You wanna order your old lady around, do what you do, not for me to say. I asked her to go, she didn’t go. Not gonna make her. But you try, you’ll deal with me.”</i>
</blockquote><br>❸ - Once Shy decided on Tab he was all in, all the way and never looked back.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“Waited for you for four years, Tabby, baby. Four. Spent a lot of that time thinkin’ I’d never have you. Now I got you, not even for a day, I’m not big on lettin’ you go. Give me that for now, yeah? Make your calls here.”</i>
</blockquote><br>❹ - Even though I want to be “no I can take care of myself” I love the way that Shy tries to look out for Tabby and take care of her and her problems, even if it isn’t exactly the way she would want him too.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>I like being in the biker world. It is a fun place to visit and although it is a harder life than I’d like in the real world in my fantasy world it totally works for me.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15009468458454153272"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415790i/820937.png' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Can someone tell me where I can found a man like Shy???? Please...!!!<br/>Tabitha is the daughter of Chaos Club President and she has been getting into trouble for three years...<br/>Shy a member of Chaos has had enough of 'Tabby Callouts' and decides to tame her wild side and teach her a lesson.Unfortunately Shy is wrong about Tabby and his lesson hurts Tabby deeply...<br/>I love that the first 15% of this book was completely from Shy's POV.It really gives us a chance to see where he is coming from and connec</span>
  <span id="freeText15009468458454153272" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415790i/820937.png" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can someone tell me where I can found a man like Shy???? Please...!!!<br>Tabitha is the daughter of Chaos Club President and she has been getting into trouble for three years...<br>Shy a member of Chaos has had enough of 'Tabby Callouts' and decides to tame her wild side and teach her a lesson.Unfortunately Shy is wrong about Tabby and his lesson hurts Tabby deeply...<br>I love that the first 15% of this book was completely from Shy's POV.It really gives us a chance to see where he is coming from and connect with him as a character We met him in Motorcycle Man &amp; knew he was a stand up guy, but we didn't really know him. Out to protect his 'family'.It's obvious to the reader that he has feelings beyond a family bond for Tabby, but of course he doesn't realize this. I think that's what makes the first chunk of this book so emotionally.Watching him struggle with his feelings, and guilt trying to do the right thing...<br>It really pained me to watch the chain of unfortunate events and time spent leading up to Shy &amp; Tabby's 'brokenness' to their bonding.<br> And when they finally came together...Holu shit!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415790ra/820938.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380415790ra/820939.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just loved Tabby and I know you will too.I loved how she dealt with being the daughter of Tack and how she did dealt with her problems. And Shy wow he is in my top 5 favorite Kristen Ashley men!!!Shy is hot, sexy, smart, loyal, loving.I can go on and on.The only problem is that he doesnt like to do laundry or vacuum I can put up with that :) :) <br>Together they are hot,intence and imotional..<br><br> "I dreamed a dream when I was sixteen and here I am, standing with my dream, feeling it come real." <br><br><br>Another amazing book from Kristen Ashley!!!<br><br><br>My Shy and Tab<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415790i/820940.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405986i/791591._SY540_.png" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415790i/820941._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4786276382127838576"><i>Review written May 5, 2016</i><br/><br/><b>3.8 Stars - Cute romantic and just the right amount of listening hours</b><br/><br/>At last the first book in this <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/92715-chaos' rel='nofollow noopener'>Chaos</a> series (loved both #2 and #4). — I bought the paperback some years ago but never got to it. A new try with a 11:30 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7412217.Angela_Starling' title='Angela Starling' rel='nofollow noopener'>Angela Starling</a>. <br/><br/>This was a good enough KA. I liked but wasn't amazed. <br/><br/>*******************************************<br/><br/><b>Tabitha 'Tabby' Allen</b> grew up in the <i>Chaos Motorcycle Club</i> as the Chaos' leader <i>Tack Allen</i>'s beloved daughter.   <span id="freeText4786276382127838576" style="display:none"><i>Review written May 5, 2016</i><br><br><b>3.8 Stars - Cute romantic and just the right amount of listening hours</b><br><br>At last the first book in this <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/92715-chaos" rel="nofollow noopener">Chaos</a> series (loved both #2 and #4). — I bought the paperback some years ago but never got to it. A new try with a 11:30 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7412217.Angela_Starling" title="Angela Starling" rel="nofollow noopener">Angela Starling</a>. <br><br>This was a good enough KA. I liked but wasn't amazed. <br><br>*******************************************<br><br><b>Tabitha 'Tabby' Allen</b> grew up in the <i>Chaos Motorcycle Club</i> as the Chaos' leader <i>Tack Allen</i>'s beloved daughter. Years passed but one rider was different from the start and he is still there. <b>Shy Cage</b> has waited for his chance to get the woman he want...<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Cars%20and%20more/image_zpsrbhqkc82.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462030805i/18946069.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsrbhqkc82.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“You’re the fuckin’ shit, Tabby.”<br>“I know,” I told him airily on another smile. “My man tells me that all the time.”<br>His eyes dropped to my mouth and his lips ordered, “Kiss me, baby.” </blockquote><br><b>Actually, it feels embarrassing</b> that we female romance books readers are so charmed by these semi-criminal motorcycle club men. Men who, all more or less, think they have the right to live by their very own rules. Yes, this is about a culture filled with goodlooking, horny sexy and badass tough men, with pretty dumb old-fashioned cavemen manners. Men that think themselves a bit god-like with women who accept much of these "man" rules way too often.<br><br><i>~ What happened to equality between sexes, democracy, and equal rights and the same law for everyone? Just wondering. ~</i> <br><br>Well, we readers accept, swallow crap and freaking keep loving these KA characters time after time. I can't but be a bit irritated about overly sweet "submissive" heroines who often are just rambling, mumbling and likes to <u>give</u> (and GIVE even more) just they get it naughty good and cozy steamy in the bed.— YEP, but nevertheless I'm charmed, mostly silly enchanted and think it's romantic as hell. — Give me mercy! I'm an incurable romantic girl. <br><br>*******************************************<br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-action.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462458393ra/19000022.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <b>I LIKE - hot <i>badass</i> bikers ...irritating but true</b><br></span>

<div id="review_465410339" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/465410339" />
    <a title="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy"><img alt="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411318166p2/7690153.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/465410339?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" href="/user/show/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy">Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=messed-up-past">messed-up-past</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=romance-angst">romance-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=panty-dropper-swoon-worthy-hot-male">panty-dropper-swoon-worthy-hot-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=bossy">bossy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=h">h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy?shelf=loanable">loanable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer465410339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5288777253445239638"><br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Parker "Shy" Cage</u>
</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><blockquote>
  <i>She pressed closer. <br/>“I dreamed a dream, Shy.” <br/>“You’ll dream more dreams, baby.” <br/>“I’ll never dream,” she whispered, her voice lost, tragic. <br/>“We’ll get you to a dream, honey,” he promised, pulling her closer.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Tabitha "Tabby" Allen</u>
</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Today, at the Compound, what you said, you did it.” <br/>“What, baby?” <br/>“I dreamed a dream.” <br/>His arms spasmed. <br/>I drifted to sleep, muttering, “You promised to get me to a dream, you got me to a dream. Thank you, ho</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5288777253445239638" style="display:none"><br><br><b>
  <u>My Parker "Shy" Cage</u>
</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><blockquote>
  <i>She pressed closer. <br>“I dreamed a dream, Shy.” <br>“You’ll dream more dreams, baby.” <br>“I’ll never dream,” she whispered, her voice lost, tragic. <br>“We’ll get you to a dream, honey,” he promised, pulling her closer.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <u>My Tabitha "Tabby" Allen</u>
</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Today, at the Compound, what you said, you did it.” <br>“What, baby?” <br>“I dreamed a dream.” <br>His arms spasmed. <br>I drifted to sleep, muttering, “You promised to get me to a dream, you got me to a dream. Thank you, honey.” <br>Then I fell asleep.</i>
</blockquote><br><br> <span>[image error]</span><br><br><br><b>This is definitly top 5 of KA</b>, for me. You would think aaaah it's a biker story: rough guys, potty mouth, loose women, tequila and bikes. And it is all that and so much more. As only KA can do, she delivered a nice emotional punch to take the wind out of you and it's not enough she brought the big guns of <i>Les Mis</i>.<br><br><b>Tabby</b> is a CHAOS daughter... born, bred and raised in the life. We see her wild side in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a>, in the story of how her dad and President of biker club, CHAOS, meets his one and only sex-kitten Tyra/Ty-Ty/Red/Cherry. Tabby parties and part of club's duty is to do <b>Tabby Call-outs</b> when things get wild and Tabby extraction is deemed necessary. One night <b>Shy</b> grows tired of if and lays it into her... HARD. So hard that not only he sets her on the right path... he puts her onto a different one where she turns into someone who is not her. That path is good and wholesome, no complains, but it is not her. I'm afraid to say it but "thankfully" fate has other plans and yanks her off that path into the void. A void of being a 23 year old with a dead fiancee. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Baby, bein’ your safe harbor doesn’t come with me gettin’ pissed when you gotta do what you gotta do when you gotta do it. It also doesn’t come with me expecting you to explain why you did what you had to do. Bein’ your safe harbor means lettin’ you do what you gotta do when you gotta do it and not gettin’ pissed.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>So, Shy gets in there and burrows deep until he find her in the most bossy, alpha, biker, yet so gently to bring back Tabby. It was cute how he thought hard ultimatums will do it, but thankfully after 2nd time he learned that that won't work on Tab. <br><br>It's an amazing ride of Shy and Tab getting to know each other, not exactly insta-romance but still is. SERIOUSLY! I love KA for giving us all these protective Alphas who can be total jerks but once they are straightened out the more I love them (Case in points my Joe obsession).<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399053ra/771817.gif" width="400" height="513" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is awesome and I LOVED IT! There are so many awesome characters who I hope to see more of... like NOW, NOW, NOW!<br><br><i>There are some great shout-outs to Rock Chicks, Mystery Man and even a smallest hint of Knight series. I freaking loved it and I loved it that my girls enjoyed it and especially my girl Jamie who got a bit of her Hawk.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5288777253445239638" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_581874588" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/581874588" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5107700-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371826269p2/5107700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/581874588?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/5107700-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer581874588" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17964068340091476543"><b>5 I Dreamed a Dream Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452545827i/17707188._SY540_.jpg' width='385"/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Shy, Shy, Shy...you are definitely not shy, which totally made my day. I was in the mood for some biker loving and you gave me exactly what I was looking for. I do have to say that Tack Allen is still my favorite Chaos member, but Shy just pulled up right behind him. If you haven't read <i>Motorcycle Man</i> you really need to. Sooooo good!<br/><br/>Parker "Shy" Cage is definitely not shy. He received his nickname for not being shy when getting around with the ladies. He is a ladies man</span>
  <span id="freeText17964068340091476543" style="display:none"><b>5 I Dreamed a Dream Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452545827i/17707188._SY540_.jpg" width='385"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Shy, Shy, Shy...you are definitely not shy, which totally made my day. I was in the mood for some biker loving and you gave me exactly what I was looking for. I do have to say that Tack Allen is still my favorite Chaos member, but Shy just pulled up right behind him. If you haven't read <i>Motorcycle Man</i> you really need to. Sooooo good!<br><br>Parker "Shy" Cage is definitely not shy. He received his nickname for not being shy when getting around with the ladies. He is a ladies man, a player, a lover. He also has noticed Tabitha Allen. Tabby is the daughter of Tack Allen, leader of the Chaos Motorcycle Club, which makes her off-limits.<br><br>Shy would do anything just like any of the other brothers in the MC would. One night Shy gets a. All that Tabby needs to be picked up. He assumes she's out partying, wasting her life away making careless decisions. When he picks her up he comes down hard on her. He's trying to get her to see that she can make something of herself if she would just try. God love him, he's coming from a good place. But he's harsh and he hurts her feelings. He doesn't let he explain the situation. <br><br>So from that point on, Tabby decides to avoid Shy. She moves on with her life. Finished nursing school. Meets a boy, falls in love and is engaged to be married. Then tragedy strikes and Tabby's fiancé is killed. All of the MC brothers are there for Tabby. They would do anything for her. Soon Shy and Tabby are spending lots of time together. They form a friendship. Shy is there for Tabby day or night. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452545827i/17707189._SY540_.jpg" width='385"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But when Tabby finds out that Shy has been dating someone, this causes a major blowup between them. Tabby is hurt again for two reasons, 1) because she thought they were friends and he didn't tell her and 2) because she was starting to have feelings for him. Shy has to go all alpha male on her and make her talk to him, but once he finds out she has feelings for him that's all it takes for him to get his life in order. He knows he's been seeing the other girl because he was looking for something, but he wasn't getting what he wanted and so he let her go. Then he and a Tabby became a couple. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Now you’re willin’ to give me more and I'm gonna take that too.”<br>"You were gone for me?"<br>"Gone for you."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>There was no denying the chemistry between them. And because of stupid communication problems these two had, they had a lot of time to make up for. I loved them as a couple. They really were good together, even arguing over cleaning. But the one thing they didn't do was tell her family or the rest of the MC family. This caused a big fight between everyone, but I loved how strong Tabby was and how she stood up for her man. Having Tack Allen as your father can't be easy, but she didn't even back down from him. Eventually things get back on track, but Tabby's friend causes problems and I mean big problems. But what motorcycle club do you know that doesn't have some type of drama? Besides, this drama lets us have some more time with Hawk, Brock and Mitch. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452545827i/17707190._SY540_.jpg" width='385"/' class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't wait to see where this series goes. Hop and Lanie are next in the series. I hope that I get more Tack Allen in each book. It only makes sense right? You can't have a book about Chaos MC and not have the leader in there somewhere. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17964068340091476543" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13044150297161995629"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399054i/771818.jpg' width='275' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I'm alive. You're alive. I gotta work to live so I do that and I'll have to do that for a long time. But when I'm not workin', I'm livin'. So lets ride."</i>
</b><br/><br/>The first half of this book was fantastic, I was glued to Tabby and Shy’s story. I enjoyed both Shy and Tabby’s povs but sadly, the second half of the book fell flat for me. It still was a good read and I did enjoy it.<br/><br/>Tabby Allen stole my heart in Motorcycle Man, she so likable and real. She is the daughter of Tack Allen (yes our Motorcycle</span>
  <span id="freeText13044150297161995629" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399054i/771818.jpg" width="275" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm alive. You're alive. I gotta work to live so I do that and I'll have to do that for a long time. But when I'm not workin', I'm livin'. So lets ride."</i>
</b><br><br>The first half of this book was fantastic, I was glued to Tabby and Shy’s story. I enjoyed both Shy and Tabby’s povs but sadly, the second half of the book fell flat for me. It still was a good read and I did enjoy it.<br><br>Tabby Allen stole my heart in Motorcycle Man, she so likable and real. She is the daughter of Tack Allen (yes our Motorcycle Man) and she has crushed on Shy for the longest time. Shy pulls a scared straight act on her and she ices him out for years. <br> <br>Tabby’s life takes a different path than that of Ride and Chaos Motorcycle Club but when tragedy strikes Shy seizes the opportunity to have Tabby Allen in his life. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I had a taste of you four years ago that I could never get off my tongue. Now, I've tasted more of you with more than just my mouth and I know I wanna keep it in a way I don't want to think of it bein' done. Not in a few weeks. Not in a few months. Maybe not ever"</i>
</b><br><br>Shy and Tabby stand up for their relationship and prove that they are in it for the long haul. The couple faces bumps in the road like family, laundry, toilet seat lids, and a drug addict best friend but they do it together. <br> <br>Loved Loved...all cameo appearances from some of my favorite characters. Hawk Delgado is still sooo yummy. You Get Me?<br><br>Overall this book was a good read. I'll be waiting with my helmet on for the next ride! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399054ra/771819.gif" width="275" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer461368176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6296925843241911883"><b>A Gazillion Stars!!! Best Book Ever!!!!</b><br/><br/>Okay people this is going to be a complete and total gush fest. I absolutely loved this book. It ranks up there in the top 5 books I have read this year. I think it is my number 2 with True Love Story still holding at number 1. <br/><br/>Tabby and Shy were just amazing together. The words on the pages were true genius. Shy was the perfect Alpha Male and Tabby was an awesome heroine. I love me some alpha male and Kristen Ashley certainly knows what she is doing when s</span>
  <span id="freeText6296925843241911883" style="display:none"><b>A Gazillion Stars!!! Best Book Ever!!!!</b><br /><br />Okay people this is going to be a complete and total gush fest. I absolutely loved this book. It ranks up there in the top 5 books I have read this year. I think it is my number 2 with True Love Story still holding at number 1. <br /><br />Tabby and Shy were just amazing together. The words on the pages were true genius. Shy was the perfect Alpha Male and Tabby was an awesome heroine. I love me some alpha male and Kristen Ashley certainly knows what she is doing when she writes one. Shy has been added to my list of book boyfriends and I have a huge fictional crush on him. It makes me wish my husband were part of a motorcycle club like Chaos and that he was an alpha male like Shy. Oh well I still love my hubby anyways. <br /><br />I have one huge complaint. This book was not long enough. It seems her last two books have been shorter than what I am used to from KA. I am accustomed to her longer books. I really hope this wont be a trend for future books. Regardless I am still in awe of this book.<br /><br />So I have a few words of advise for my fellow readers. If you haven't read this book. Stop the book you are reading and pick this one up. It is amazing. KA at her finest. <b>Truly a must read people</b> I have no doubt you will fall in love with Tabby and Shy as I have. Truly a brilliant book!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="6296925843241911883" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_532727628" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532727628" />
    <a title="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina"><img alt="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1418082097p2/5897822.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532727628?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" href="/user/show/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina">Michele ~ la Smoocherina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=made-my-heart-sing">made-my-heart-sing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=emotionally-satisfying">emotionally-satisfying</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=omg-i-loved-it">omg-i-loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=can-t-keep-their-hands-off-each-oth">can-t-keep-their-hands-off-each-oth</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=couldn-t-put-it-down">couldn-t-put-it-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=tattoo">tattoo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=features-a-good-father">features-a-good-father</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=good-dirty-talk-or-phone-sex">good-dirty-talk-or-phone-sex</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532727628" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer27306612482418950">Great job Kit! I am very impressed! I admit, I was worried when Kristen Ashley went from self-published to professionally published, but I must say they did not take away the magic of Kristen Ashley. If anything, they made it better.<br/><br/>So I'm going to give it to you nugget style. :)<br/><br/>What I loved-<br/><br/>-Shy was Alpha, but not the Über-Alpha we've come to associate with Kristen Ashley. He listened to his woman, cared for her input. There were times when he brooked not argument, don't get me wrong, but he wa</span>
  <span id="freeText27306612482418950" style="display:none">Great job Kit! I am very impressed! I admit, I was worried when Kristen Ashley went from self-published to professionally published, but I must say they did not take away the magic of Kristen Ashley. If anything, they made it better.<br /><br />So I'm going to give it to you nugget style. :)<br /><br />What I loved-<br /><br />-Shy was Alpha, but not the Über-Alpha we've come to associate with Kristen Ashley. He listened to his woman, cared for her input. There were times when he brooked not argument, don't get me wrong, but he wanted the sweetness his parents had together for himself and it only made him a sexier hero in my opinion. He loved Tabby fiercely, even when they were just friends. Push comes to shove, he'd pick Tabby over everything, including Chaos.<br /><br />-Tabby is a nurse. I know a thing or two about this. I found she was one of the most level, drama free heroines KA has written. I loved her. Her intelligence. Her sweetness. The fact that she owned her "biker babe since birth" status and loved to be on the back of a bike. Her desire to be kind and helpful. She reminded me a bit of Tess that way. All that said, she put her foot down also, when it mattered. But stood by her man when it counted. She was brave, took chances and loved with everything in her. Great heroine!<br /><br />-We get some Tack! Oh yes. Tack. Love him, he's a grade-A man and father. He treats his adult children with respect and models love in the best way.<br /><br />-<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[We get Elvira and her man. It's a small bit, but as with anything Elvira, it's AWESOME! We also get some of the characters from Rock Chick and the Dream Man Series. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />-This book had a good plot. Believable even. It wasn't filled with the big boom of kidnapping, rape and such that a lot of KA books do, but I can sense the big boom will come sometime in the series.<br /><br />-Condoms were used and a discussion about safe sex took place. Thank you Kit! *twirly dance* (The lack of safe sex practice in past KA books has really bothered me. I felt good that Shy gloved up!)<br /><br />-Alternating POV. Fantastic! I loved it!<br /><br />-Shy's brother Lan. I hope he gets a book. He's wonderful!<br /><br />-Character growth. Gotta love it.<br /><br />-Shy's sweet talk. When he puts it all on the line, it will make you swoon.<br /><br />-We get to see the beginning of Hop and Lanie's book. I didn't think I could like Hop due to the whole BeeBee thing. But I do. KA made it happen.<br /><br />-I could go on and on, but really, it was just great.<br /><br />What I didn't like-<br /><br />-This has to do with me being a nurse, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Tabby had issues with Dr. Dickhead riding her at work. So bad, she considered quitting. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Then Shy had to take matters into the clubs hands, which is ridiculous.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'm not saying doctors aren't dicks, because they can be. But gone are the days when that was tolerated. Doctors and nurses are colleagues. Nurses aren't doctor's handmaidens anymore. Abuse gets reported. But I get why KA wrote that. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It made for good plot.<br /><br />-Where's my kickass epilogue? It was just a few pages.<br /><br />Definite recommended read. <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="27306612482418950" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
