<div id="review_560755102" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/560755102" />
    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451733481p2/2367556.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/560755102?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560755102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5306402295094415666"><b>I LOVED every moment of this book. Tab and Shy were the BEST KA characters of this series!!!<br/><br/>This is one of the BEST book's I've EVER read!!<br/> <br/>Story Rating 5 Stars<br/>Character Rating 5 Stars<br/>Romance Rating 5 Stars<br/>Heat Level 4 Stars<br/>Overall Rating 5 Stars<br/> <br/>I have to say that out of all of Kristen Ashley's books that I have read that this one is Hands down the BEST!! When I say the BEST I mean the BEST story line, The BEST characters, the BEST romance, the BEST dialogue, the MOST heat, it was just out of t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5306402295094415666" style="display:none"><b>I LOVED every moment of this book. Tab and Shy were the BEST KA characters of this series!!!<br /><br />This is one of the BEST book's I've EVER read!!<br /> <br />Story Rating 5 Stars<br />Character Rating 5 Stars<br />Romance Rating 5 Stars<br />Heat Level 4 Stars<br />Overall Rating 5 Stars<br /> <br />I have to say that out of all of Kristen Ashley's books that I have read that this one is Hands down the BEST!! When I say the BEST I mean the BEST story line, The BEST characters, the BEST romance, the BEST dialogue, the MOST heat, it was just out of this world FANTASTIC. Can you feel me?<br /> <br />Right from the beginning I was drawn into the story. It took us on a huge journey of how these two got together and let me tell you, that was not an easy road and it did not happen easily. They were not just thrown together like we read in most romances. Once they finally realized how much they meant to each other it was absolutely WONDERFUL. <br /> <br />OMG, how I LOVED SHY. He was everything my dream man would be and so much more. Kind, gentle, caring, protective, honorable, SEXY, demanding, oh yes, he was VERY demanding in more ways than one. I know it's hard to believe that any woman would be able to tame this sexy man. He had woman falling all over him and he would take it when he could get it and as many women he could. When he finally realized that Tabby had deep feeling for him, he totally made an about face, got rid of the other woman and gave everything to her, EVERYTHING! The dialoged these two had for each other was the most romantic stuff I've EVER READ! When I say you could feel the love between them, you REALLY could feel the love between them. It flew off of the pages and into my heart.<br /> <br />I loved Tabby every bit as much as Shy. She had something terrible happen to her that was devastating. It was wonderful reading how Shy helped her over come this and how they became close friends and then later lovers. When push came to shove she was fearless and stood by her man defying EVERYONE for the love she felt for Shy. WOW, you all so going to LOVE this book.<br /> <br />Kristen Ashley also turned the heat up in this one. When these two hit the sheets, counters, floor, wherever they could get their hands, mouths and other body parts moving together it was Spectacular. <br /> <br />I know this review can NO way explain to you just how much I LOVED this book. I only hope that you really can feel me and you buy this book and read it for yourself. Mark my words, once it releases it's going to be a HUGE success. DO NOT let it sit there, pick it up and find out just why all of us woman at Swept Away By Romance were completely BLOWN AWAY by this book.</b><br /><br /><br /><i>**ARC kindly provided to Swept Away By Romance courtesy of Grand Central Publishing, Kristen Ashley and Chas**</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5306402295094415666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pFoWrHvSZVsaZmrnR/YFD64wiWifF2SZlon3GAP6yCyBQkIODLYvqv29IldMErBxIF7pYY70Vb0SuKHUnAKxXw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mJsroOgSnaZ/Inel/woRmmra6qJgNuGll5lVcI5A68y9g38Cn3bXV5j5PxX07qTk5LSKq3HV0IETqAO8EbiSvw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer3731504585842591392">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText3731504585842591392" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
